// FILE: NHL.SemanticModel\definition\expressions.tmdl

expression fxGetPlayByPlay = ```
		(GameID as text) =>
		let
		    // 1. Base API config
		    BaseUrl = "https://api-web.nhle.com",
		    Path = "v1/gamecenter/" & Text.Trim(GameID) & "/play-by-play",
		
		    // 2. Fetch JSON with a User-Agent header to prevent silent server blocking
		    Source = try Json.Document(Web.Contents(BaseUrl, [RelativePath=Path, Headers=[#"User-Agent"="PowerBI"]])) otherwise null,
		
		    // 3. Extract plays safely
		    PlaysList = if Source <> null and Record.HasFields(Source, "plays") then Source[plays] else {},
		    PlaysTable = Table.FromList(PlaysList, Splitter.SplitByNothing(), {"Column1"}, null, ExtraValues.Error),
		
		    // 4. Branch logic: If empty, return strict schema. If populated, parse safely.
		    Result = if Table.IsEmpty(PlaysTable) then
		        #table(
		            type table [GameID=text, EventID=text, PeriodNumber=Int64.Type, TimeInPeriod_Seconds=Int64.Type, EventType=text, EventTeamID=Int64.Type, X_Coord=number, Y_Coord=number, ScoringPlayerID=Int64.Type, ShootingPlayerID=Int64.Type, HittingPlayerID=Int64.Type, HitteePlayerID=Int64.Type],
		            {}
		        )
		    else let
		        // FIX: Sanitize nodes to ensure they are records before expanding.
		        // This prevents dirty API data (like []) from destroying the entire column schema.
		        SanitizedRoot = Table.TransformColumns(PlaysTable, {{"Column1", each if _ is record then _ else null}}),
		        ExpandedPlays = Table.ExpandRecordColumn(SanitizedRoot, "Column1", 
		            {"eventId", "periodDescriptor", "timeInPeriod", "typeDescKey", "details"}, 
		            {"EventID", "PeriodRecord", "TimeInPeriod", "EventType", "DetailsRecord"}
		        ),
		
		        SanitizedPeriod = Table.TransformColumns(ExpandedPlays, {{"PeriodRecord", each if _ is record then _ else null}}),
		        ExpandedPeriod = Table.ExpandRecordColumn(SanitizedPeriod, "PeriodRecord", {"number"}, {"PeriodNumber"}),
		
		        SanitizedDetails = Table.TransformColumns(ExpandedPeriod, {{"DetailsRecord", each if _ is record then _ else null}}),
		        ExpandedDetails = Table.ExpandRecordColumn(SanitizedDetails, "DetailsRecord", 
		            {"xCoord", "yCoord", "eventOwnerTeamId", "scoringPlayerId", "shootingPlayerId", "hittingPlayerId", "hitteePlayerId"}, 
		            {"X_Coord", "Y_Coord", "EventTeamID", "ScoringPlayerID", "ShootingPlayerID", "HittingPlayerID", "HitteePlayerID"}
		        ),
		
		        // 5. Time calculation safely handling nulls
		        SplitTime = Table.SplitColumn(ExpandedDetails, "TimeInPeriod", Splitter.SplitTextByDelimiter(":", QuoteStyle.Csv), {"Minute", "Second"}),
		        ChangedTimeTypes = Table.TransformColumnTypes(SplitTime, {{"Minute", Int64.Type}, {"Second", Int64.Type}}),
		        AddSeconds = Table.AddColumn(ChangedTimeTypes, "TimeInPeriod_Seconds", 
		            each if [Minute] <> null and [Second] <> null then ([Minute] * 60) + [Second] else null, 
		            Int64.Type
		        ),
		
		        AddGameID = Table.AddColumn(AddSeconds, "GameID", each GameID, type text),
		
		        // 6. Strict column selection mapping ensuring all columns pass through
		        FinalColumns = Table.SelectColumns(AddGameID, 
		            {"GameID", "EventID", "PeriodNumber", "TimeInPeriod_Seconds", "EventType", "EventTeamID", "X_Coord", "Y_Coord", "ScoringPlayerID", "ShootingPlayerID", "HittingPlayerID", "HitteePlayerID"}, 
		            MissingField.UseNull
		        )
		    in
		        FinalColumns
		in
		    Result
		```
	lineageTag: aad82752-9c50-4b4d-85e4-623bf62c6939

	annotation PBI_NavigationStepName = Navigation

	annotation PBI_ResultType = Function

expression fxGetPlayerEDGE = ```
		(InputPlayerID as text) =>
		let
		    // 1. Static Base URL and RelativePath configuration
		    BaseUrl = "https://api-web.nhle.com",
		    
		    // FIX: Update URL path to 20252026
		    Path = "v1/edge/skater-skating-speed-detail/" & InputPlayerID & "/20252026/2",
		
		    // 2. API Governance: Implement implicit rate limiting
		    SourceData = Function.InvokeAfter(
		        () => try Json.Document(Web.Contents(BaseUrl, [RelativePath=Path])) otherwise null,
		        #duration(0, 0, 0, 0.3)
		    ),
		
		    // 3. Extract the exact parent nodes
		    TopSpeedsNode = try SourceData[topSkatingSpeeds] otherwise null,
		    SpeedDetailsNode = try SourceData[skatingSpeedDetails] otherwise null,
		
		    // 4. Create a clean, flat record
		    FlatRecord = [
		        PlayerID = InputPlayerID, 
		        TopSkatingSpeeds = TopSpeedsNode,
		        SkatingSpeedDetails = SpeedDetailsNode
		    ],
		
		    // 5. Convert to Table
		    DataTable = Table.FromRecords({FlatRecord}),
		
		    // 6. Data Typing
		    TypedData = Table.TransformColumnTypes(DataTable, {
		        {"PlayerID", Int64.Type}
		    })
		in
		    TypedData
		```
	lineageTag: b5850f58-7435-4a8a-aaa3-16adbcb82de1

	annotation PBI_NavigationStepName = Navigation

	annotation PBI_ResultType = Function

expression Staging_EDGE = ```
		let
		    // 1. Reference the existing Dimension table to get the active Player IDs
		    Source = DimPlayers,
		    
		    // 2. Remove all descriptive columns to keep this table lightweight
		    // We only need the PlayerID to feed into our custom function
		    IsolatedIDs = Table.SelectColumns(Source,{"PlayerID"}),
		    
		    // 3. Convert PlayerID to Text temporarily to match the function parameter
		    ChangedType = Table.TransformColumnTypes(IsolatedIDs,{{"PlayerID", type text}}),
		    
		    // 4. Invoke the EDGE API function
		    // WARNING: Due to the 300ms delay to prevent rate-limiting, this step will take 3-4 minutes to process all ~700 players.
		    InvokedFunction = Table.AddColumn(ChangedType, "EDGE_Data", each fxGetPlayerEDGE([PlayerID])),
		    #"Expanded EDGE_Data" = Table.ExpandTableColumn(InvokedFunction, "EDGE_Data", {"TopSkatingSpeeds", "SkatingSpeedDetails"}, {"TopSkatingSpeeds", "SkatingSpeedDetails"})
		in
		    #"Expanded EDGE_Data"
		```
	lineageTag: b2c4d25b-bac2-44d1-8f34-a785c8ab9764

	annotation PBI_NavigationStepName = Navigation

	annotation PBI_ResultType = Exception

expression game =
		let
		    Source = Csv.Document(File.Contents("C:\Users\herblize\Downloads\archive\game.csv"),[Delimiter=",", Columns=15, Encoding=1252, QuoteStyle=QuoteStyle.None]),
		    #"Promoted Headers" = Table.PromoteHeaders(Source, [PromoteAllScalars=true]),
		    #"Changed Type" = Table.TransformColumnTypes(#"Promoted Headers",{{"game_id", Int64.Type}, {"season", Int64.Type}, {"type", type text}, {"date_time_GMT", type datetime}, {"away_team_id", Int64.Type}, {"home_team_id", Int64.Type}, {"away_goals", Int64.Type}, {"home_goals", Int64.Type}, {"outcome", type text}, {"home_rink_side_start", type text}, {"venue", type text}, {"venue_link", type text}, {"venue_time_zone_id", type text}, {"venue_time_zone_offset", Int64.Type}, {"venue_time_zone_tz", type text}})
		in
		    #"Changed Type"
	lineageTag: db2029b9-16ba-4b52-99d8-111f569d30c2

	annotation PBI_NavigationStepName = Navigation

	annotation PBI_ResultType = Table

table DimGames
	lineageTag: bbd493a1-8060-4baa-bbb9-66318297a19c

	column GameID
		dataType: int64
		formatString: 0
		lineageTag: 1535b46e-829f-4566-9454-5ab5e6d014c0
		summarizeBy: none
		sourceColumn: GameID

		annotation SummarizationSetBy = Automatic

	column Season
		dataType: int64
		formatString: 0
		lineageTag: 7c0109c9-19fa-4a87-b54e-fd95eff202d5
		summarizeBy: sum
		sourceColumn: Season

		annotation SummarizationSetBy = Automatic

	column GameType
		dataType: string
		lineageTag: 6821dd76-31c8-4dbe-be5f-9058d66b4b75

		annotation SummarizationSetBy = Automatic

		dataType: dateTime
		formatString: Long Date
		lineageTag: c23d9f0b-bdd1-4042-8d64-cd2c559cced3

	column HomeTeamID
		dataType: int64
		formatString: 0
		lineageTag: 613170b9-5d36-48ba-89af-cf27ea9d7b09
		summarizeBy: count
		sourceColumn: HomeTeamID

		annotation SummarizationSetBy = Automatic

	column HomeTeamAbbrev
		dataType: string
		lineageTag: 1bee5ce5-3bf9-4ad6-ad63-85cfc9b6a8c6
		summarizeBy: none
		sourceColumn: HomeTeamAbbrev

		annotation SummarizationSetBy = Automatic

	column HomeScore
		dataType: string
		lineageTag: 3aa7a795-6416-404f-b3eb-d7143542999e
		summarizeBy: none
		sourceColumn: HomeScore

		annotation SummarizationSetBy = Automatic

	column AwayTeamID
		dataType: int64
		formatString: 0
		lineageTag: c7396bca-7e14-4f05-b144-b7b814608a63
		summarizeBy: count
		sourceColumn: AwayTeamID

		annotation SummarizationSetBy = Automatic

	column AwayTeamAbbrev
		dataType: string
		lineageTag: b219ff76-8a60-42c9-be0a-31671627f054
		summarizeBy: none
		sourceColumn: AwayTeamAbbrev

		annotation SummarizationSetBy = Automatic

	column AwayScore
		dataType: string
		lineageTag: 14f6319e-9d48-4d51-9d2f-a91db59d513b
		summarizeBy: none
		sourceColumn: AwayScore

		annotation SummarizationSetBy = Automatic

	partition DimGames = m
		mode: import
		source = ```
				let
				    // --- BRANCH A: LIVE GAMES (FULL 2025-2026 SEASON) ---
				    BaseUrl = "https://api-web.nhle.com",
				    
				    // 1. Create a master list of all 32 NHL Teams (Including UTA for Utah)
				    TeamsList = {"ANA", "BOS", "BUF", "CAR", "CBJ", "CGY", "CHI", "COL", "DAL", "DET", "EDM", "FLA", "LAK", "MIN", "MTL", "NJD", "NSH", "NYI", "NYR", "OTT", "PHI", "PIT", "SEA", "SJS", "STL", "TBL", "TOR", "UTA", "VAN", "VGK", "WPG", "WSH"},
				    TeamsTable = Table.FromList(TeamsList, Splitter.SplitByNothing(), {"TeamAbbrev"}, null, ExtraValues.Error),
				
				    // 2. Fetch the full 2025-2026 schedule for EVERY team
				    FetchSchedules = Table.AddColumn(TeamsTable, "ScheduleData", each
				        try Json.Document(Web.Contents(BaseUrl, [RelativePath="v1/club-schedule-season/" & [TeamAbbrev] & "/20252026", Headers=[#"User-Agent"="PowerBI"]])) otherwise null
				    ),
				
				    // 3. Filter out any API hiccups, then expand the 'games' array
				    RemoveNullSchedules = Table.SelectRows(FetchSchedules, each ([ScheduleData] <> null and Record.HasFields([ScheduleData], "games"))),
				    ExpandedGamesList = Table.ExpandRecordColumn(RemoveNullSchedules, "ScheduleData", {"games"}, {"games"}),
				    ExpandedGamesArray = Table.ExpandListColumn(ExpandedGamesList, "games"),
				
				    // 4. Safely expand the individual game records
				    RemoveBlankGames = Table.SelectRows(ExpandedGamesArray, each [games] <> null),
				    ExpandedGames = Table.ExpandRecordColumn(RemoveBlankGames, "games", 
				        {"id", "season", "gameType", "gameDate", "gameState", "homeTeam", "awayTeam"}, 
				        {"GameID", "Season", "GameType", "GameDate", "GameState", "HomeTeamRecord", "AwayTeamRecord"}
				    ),
				
				    // 5. Safely expand Home and Away team details (Future games might not have a 'score' node yet, this prevents crashing)
				    SanitizedHome = Table.TransformColumns(ExpandedGames, {{"HomeTeamRecord", each if _ is record then _ else null}}),
				    ExpandedHome = Table.ExpandRecordColumn(SanitizedHome, "HomeTeamRecord", {"id", "abbrev", "score"}, {"HomeTeamID", "HomeTeamAbbrev", "HomeScore"}),
				
				    SanitizedAway = Table.TransformColumns(ExpandedHome, {{"AwayTeamRecord", each if _ is record then _ else null}}),
				    ExpandedAway = Table.ExpandRecordColumn(SanitizedAway, "AwayTeamRecord", {"id", "abbrev", "score"}, {"AwayTeamID", "AwayTeamAbbrev", "AwayScore"}),
				
				    // 6. Select and format the Live Branch columns
				    LiveGames = Table.SelectColumns(ExpandedAway, {"GameID", "Season", "GameType", "GameDate", "GameState", "HomeTeamID", "HomeTeamAbbrev", "HomeScore", "AwayTeamID", "AwayTeamAbbrev", "AwayScore"}, MissingField.Ignore),
				    CleanedLive = Table.TransformColumnTypes(LiveGames, {
				        {"GameID", Int64.Type}, {"Season", Int64.Type}, {"GameType", type text}, {"GameDate", type date}, 
				        {"GameState", type text}, {"HomeTeamID", Int64.Type}, {"AwayTeamID", Int64.Type}
				    }),
				
				    // --- BRANCH B: HISTORICAL GAMES (KAGGLE) ---
				    // Extract only the necessary columns from the 'game' table and rename them to match the API
				    HistoricalGames = Table.RenameColumns(
				        Table.SelectColumns(game, {"game_id", "season", "type", "date_time_GMT", "home_team_id", "away_team_id"}, MissingField.Ignore), 
				        {{"game_id", "GameID"}, {"season", "Season"}, {"type", "GameType"}, {"date_time_GMT", "GameDate"}, {"home_team_id", "HomeTeamID"}, {"away_team_id", "AwayTeamID"}},
				        MissingField.Ignore
				    ),
				    CleanedHist = Table.TransformColumnTypes(HistoricalGames, {{"GameDate", type date}}),
				
				    // --- THE UNION ---
				    AppendedGames = try Table.Combine({CleanedLive, CleanedHist}) otherwise CleanedLive,
				
				    // Ensure final strict typing for relationships
				    TypedData = Table.TransformColumnTypes(AppendedGames, {
				        {"GameID", Int64.Type},
				        {"Season", Int64.Type},
				        {"GameDate", type date},
				        {"HomeTeamID", Int64.Type},
				        {"AwayTeamID", Int64.Type}
				    }),
				    
				    // --- ENFORCE PRIMARY KEY UNIQUENESS ---
				    // This physically removes the duplicate games generated by querying all 32 teams 
				    // and ensures DimGames acts as a flawless 1-to-Many Dimension table.
				    RemovedDuplicates = Table.Distinct(TypedData, {"GameID"}),
				    #"Sorted Rows" = Table.Sort(RemovedDuplicates,{{"GameID", Order.Descending}})
				in
				    #"Sorted Rows"
				```

	annotation PBI_NavigationStepName = Navigation

	annotation PBI_ResultType = Table

	partition DimPlayers = m
		mode: import
		source = ```
				let
				    // 1. Static Base URL and RelativePath configuration
				    BaseUrl = "https://api.nhle.com",
				    Path = "stats/rest/en/skater/summary",
				    
				    // 2. API Governance: Pull active skaters for the current 2025-2026 season
				    QueryParams = [
				        limit = "-1",
				        cayenneExp = "seasonId=20252026"
				    ],
				
				    // 3. Error Resilience: Fetch JSON
				    Source = try Json.Document(Web.Contents(BaseUrl, [RelativePath=Path, Query=QueryParams])) otherwise null,
				    DataList = try Source[data] otherwise {},
				    PlayersTable = Table.FromList(DataList, Splitter.SplitByNothing(), {"Column1"}, null, ExtraValues.Error),
				    
				    // Expand the core player attributes
				    ExpandedPlayers = try Table.ExpandRecordColumn(PlayersTable, "Column1", 
				        {"playerId", "skaterFullName", "positionCode", "shootsCatches", "gamesPlayed", "goals", "assists", "points", "teamAbbrevs"}, 
				        {"PlayerID", "PlayerName", "Position", "ShootsCatches", "GamesPlayed", "Goals", "Assists", "Points", "RawTeams"}
				    ) otherwise PlayersTable,
				
				    // Extract the current team (handling traded players gracefully)
				    AddCurrentTeam = Table.AddColumn(ExpandedPlayers, "CurrentTeamAbbrev", 
				        each try Text.Trim(Text.Split([RawTeams], ","){0}) otherwise [RawTeams], type text),
				
				    // --- THE ASSET SERVER FIX ---
				    // Construct the new mandatory CDN path utilizing the Season and Team Abbreviation
				    AddHeadshotURL = Table.AddColumn(AddCurrentTeam, "HeadshotURL", 
				        each "https://assets.nhle.com/mugs/nhl/20252026/" & [CurrentTeamAbbrev] & "/" & Text.From([PlayerID]) & ".png", type text),
				
				    // Memory Efficiency & Deduplication
				    FinalColumns = Table.SelectColumns(AddHeadshotURL, {"PlayerID", "PlayerName", "Position", "ShootsCatches", "GamesPlayed", "Goals", "Assists", "Points", "CurrentTeamAbbrev", "HeadshotURL"}, MissingField.Ignore),
				    RemoveDuplicates = Table.Distinct(FinalColumns, {"PlayerID"}),
				
				    // Strict Data Typing
				    TypedData = Table.TransformColumnTypes(RemoveDuplicates, {
				        {"PlayerID", Int64.Type}, 
				        {"PlayerName", type text}, 
				        {"Position", type text}, 
				        {"ShootsCatches", type text},
				        {"GamesPlayed", Int64.Type},
				        {"Goals", Int64.Type},
				        {"Assists", Int64.Type},
				        {"Points", Int64.Type},
				        {"CurrentTeamAbbrev", type text},
				        {"HeadshotURL", type text}
				    })
				in
				    TypedData
				```

	partition DimTeams = m
		mode: import
		source = ```
				let
				    // --- 1. CORE TEAM IDs (Required for mapping Kaggle historical IDs) ---
				    CoreUrl = "https://api.nhle.com",
				    CorePath = "stats/rest/en/team",
				    CoreParams = [limit = "-1"],
				    CoreSource = try Json.Document(Web.Contents(CoreUrl, [RelativePath=CorePath, Query=CoreParams])) otherwise null,
				    CoreList = try CoreSource[data] otherwise {},
				    CoreTable = Table.FromList(CoreList, Splitter.SplitByNothing(), {"Column1"}, null, ExtraValues.Error),
				    ExpandedCore = try Table.ExpandRecordColumn(CoreTable, "Column1", 
				        {"id", "franchiseId", "fullName", "triCode"}, 
				        {"TeamID", "FranchiseID", "TeamName", "TeamAbbrev"}
				    ) otherwise CoreTable,
				    
				    // --- 2. RICH STANDINGS DATA (Live Conference, Division, Rank, Streaks) ---
				    StandUrl = "https://api-web.nhle.com",
				    StandPath = "v1/standings/now",
				    StandSource = try Json.Document(Web.Contents(StandUrl, [RelativePath=StandPath])) otherwise null,
				    StandList = try StandSource[standings] otherwise {},
				    StandTable = Table.FromList(StandList, Splitter.SplitByNothing(), {"Column1"}, null, ExtraValues.Error),
				    
				    ExpandedStandings = try Table.ExpandRecordColumn(StandTable, "Column1", 
				        {"teamAbbrev", "conferenceName", "divisionName", "leagueSequence", "points", "streakCode", "streakCount", "goalDifferential"}, 
				        {"teamAbbrevRec", "Conference", "Division", "LeagueRank", "Points", "StreakType", "StreakCount", "GoalDifferential"}
				    ) otherwise StandTable,
				    
				    // Extract the text abbreviation from the nested record {"default": "BOS"}
				    ExtractStandingsAbbrev = try Table.ExpandRecordColumn(ExpandedStandings, "teamAbbrevRec", {"default"}, {"TeamAbbrev"}) otherwise ExpandedStandings,
				    
				    // --- 3. THE MERGE (Stitching the two APIs together) ---
				    // LeftOuter Join ensures defunct/relocated teams still exist for historical game mapping
				    MergedTeams = Table.NestedJoin(ExpandedCore, {"TeamAbbrev"}, ExtractStandingsAbbrev, {"TeamAbbrev"}, "StandingsData", JoinKind.LeftOuter),
				    ExpandedMerge = Table.ExpandTableColumn(MergedTeams, "StandingsData", 
				        {"Conference", "Division", "LeagueRank", "Points", "StreakType", "StreakCount", "GoalDifferential"}, 
				        {"Conference", "Division", "LeagueRank", "Points", "StreakType", "StreakCount", "GoalDifferential"}
				    ),
				
				    // --- 4. DATA ENHANCEMENT & TYPING ---
				    // Synthesize the official NHL SVG Logo URL
				    AddLogoURL = Table.AddColumn(ExpandedMerge, "TeamLogoURL", 
				        each "https://assets.nhle.com/logos/nhl/svg/" & [TeamAbbrev] & "_light.svg", 
				        type text
				    ),
				    
				    // Cast for optimal DAX engine performance
				    TypedData = Table.TransformColumnTypes(AddLogoURL, {
				        {"TeamID", Int64.Type}, 
				        {"FranchiseID", Int64.Type}, 
				        {"TeamName", type text}, 
				        {"TeamAbbrev", type text},
				        {"Conference", type text},
				        {"Division", type text},
				        {"LeagueRank", Int64.Type},
				        {"Points", Int64.Type},
				        {"StreakType", type text},
				        {"StreakCount", Int64.Type},
				        {"GoalDifferential", Int64.Type},
				        {"TeamLogoURL", type text}
				    }),
				
				    // --- THE FIX: ENFORCE UNIQUE ABBREVIATIONS ---
				    // The NHL stats API returns legacy duplicates for some abbreviations.
				    // We must remove duplicates so this column can act as a 1-side key in the Star Schema.
				    RemovedDuplicates = Table.Distinct(TypedData, {"TeamAbbrev"})
				in
				    RemovedDuplicates
				```

				    // SURGICAL EXTRACTION: Use a safer method to grab only the 'count' value if it's a record
				    GetCount = (val) => if val is record then try val[count] otherwise 0 else val,
				
				    AddOver22 = Table.TransformColumns(#"Expanded", {{"burstsOver22", each GetCount(_)}}),
				    Add20To22 = Table.TransformColumns(AddOver22, {{"bursts20To22", each GetCount(_)}}),
				    Add18To20 = Table.TransformColumns(Add20To22, {{"bursts18To20", each GetCount(_)}}),

				    #"ExpandedMax" = Table.ExpandRecordColumn(Add18To20, "maxSkatingSpeed", {"imperial", "leagueAvg"}),

				    // Final Strict Typing
				    Typed = Table.TransformColumnTypes(#"ExpandedAvg", {

				        {"imperial", type number},
				        {"avg.imp", type number},
				        {"burstsOver22", Int64.Type},
				        {"bursts20To22", Int64.Type},
				        {"bursts18To20", Int64.Type}
				    }),
				
				    FinalRenamed = Table.RenameColumns(Typed, {
				        {"imperial", "SkatingSpeedDetails.maxSkatingSpeed.imperial"},
				        {"avg.imp", "SkatingSpeedDetails.maxSkatingSpeed.leagueAvg.imperial"}

	partition FactHistoricalPlays = m
		mode: import
		source = ```
				let
				    // 1. Source the local Kaggle CSV file
				    Source = Csv.Document(File.Contents("C:\Users\herblize\Downloads\archive\game_plays.csv"),[Delimiter=",", Columns=18, Encoding=1252, QuoteStyle=QuoteStyle.None]),
				    PromotedHeaders = Table.PromoteHeaders(Source, [PromoteAllScalars=true]),
				    
				    // 3. Rename columns
				    RenamedColumns = Table.RenameColumns(PromotedHeaders,{
				        {"game_id", "GameID"}, {"play_id", "EventID"}, {"period", "PeriodNumber"}, 
				        {"event", "EventType"}, {"team_id_for", "EventTeamID"}, {"x", "X_Coord"}, {"y", "Y_Coord"}
				    }, MissingField.Ignore),
				    
				    #"Filtered Rows" = Table.SelectRows(RenamedColumns, each ([EventType] <> "Game End" and [EventType] <> "Game Official" and [EventType] <> "Game Scheduled" and [EventType] <> "Period End" and [EventType] <> "Period Official" and [EventType] <> "Period Ready" and [EventType] <> "Period Start" and [EventType] <> "Shootout Complete" and [EventType] <> "Stoppage") and ([X_Coord] <> "NA")),
				    
				    // 4. Time Conversion
				    SplitTime = Table.SplitColumn(#"Filtered Rows", "periodTime", Splitter.SplitTextByDelimiter(":", QuoteStyle.Csv), {"Minute", "Second"}),
				    ChangedTimeTypes = Table.TransformColumnTypes(SplitTime, {{"Minute", Int64.Type}, {"Second", Int64.Type}}),
				    AddSeconds = Table.AddColumn(ChangedTimeTypes, "TimeInPeriod_Seconds", each try ([Minute] * 60) + [Second] otherwise null, Int64.Type),
				    
				    // 5. Select unified columns
				    FinalColumns = Table.SelectColumns(AddSeconds, 
				        {"GameID", "EventID", "PeriodNumber", "TimeInPeriod_Seconds", "EventType", "EventTeamID", "X_Coord", "Y_Coord"}, MissingField.Ignore
				    ),
				
				    // 6. Scrub "NA"
				    CleanedNAs = Table.ReplaceValue(FinalColumns, "NA", null, Replacer.ReplaceValue, {"EventTeamID", "X_Coord", "Y_Coord"}),
				    
				    // 7. Inject missing columns including our new PlayerID
				    AddScoring = Table.AddColumn(CleanedNAs, "ScoringPlayerID", each null, Int64.Type),
				    AddShooting = Table.AddColumn(AddScoring, "ShootingPlayerID", each null, Int64.Type),
				    AddHitting = Table.AddColumn(AddShooting, "HittingPlayerID", each null, Int64.Type),
				    AddHittee = Table.AddColumn(AddHitting, "HitteePlayerID", each null, Int64.Type),
				    AddPlayerID = Table.AddColumn(AddHittee, "PlayerID", each null, Int64.Type),
				
				    // 8. Force exact column order to match FactLivePlays perfectly
				    ReorderedColumns = Table.ReorderColumns(AddPlayerID, 
				        {"GameID", "EventID", "PeriodNumber", "TimeInPeriod_Seconds", "EventType", "EventTeamID", "X_Coord", "Y_Coord", "PlayerID", "ScoringPlayerID", "ShootingPlayerID", "HittingPlayerID", "HitteePlayerID"}
				    ),
				
				    // 9. Strict Data Typing
				    TypedData = Table.TransformColumnTypes(ReorderedColumns,{
				        {"GameID", Int64.Type}, {"EventID", type text}, {"PeriodNumber", Int64.Type}, 
				        {"TimeInPeriod_Seconds", Int64.Type}, {"EventType", type text}, {"EventTeamID", Int64.Type}, 
				        {"X_Coord", type number}, {"Y_Coord", type number}, {"PlayerID", Int64.Type}, 
				        {"ScoringPlayerID", Int64.Type}, {"ShootingPlayerID", Int64.Type}, 
				        {"HittingPlayerID", Int64.Type}, {"HitteePlayerID", Int64.Type}
				    })
				in
				    TypedData
				```

table _Measures
	lineageTag: a1b2c3d4-e5f6-7a8b-9c0d-1e2f3a4b5c6d

	measure 'Team Points' = SUM('DimTeams'[Points])
		formatString: 0
		lineageTag: d4c3b2a1-f6e5-b8a7-d0c9-c6b5a4f3e2d1

	measure 'Team Goal Diff' = SUM('DimTeams'[GoalDifferential])
		formatString: +0;-0;0
		lineageTag: 1a2b3c4d-5e6f-7a8b-9c0d-e1f2a3b4c5d6

	measure 'Current Streak' =
			IF(
			    ISINSCOPE('DimTeams'[TeamName]),
			    MAX('DimTeams'[StreakType]) & MAX('DimTeams'[StreakCount]),
			    BLANK()
			)
		lineageTag: 9f8e7d6c-5b4a-3f2e-1d0c-b9a8f7e6d5c4

	measure 'Player Max Speed (mph)' = AVERAGE('FactEdgeBurstDetails'[SkatingSpeedDetails.maxSkatingSpeed.imperial])
		formatString: 0.00
		lineageTag: 2b3c4d5e-6f7a-8b9c-0d1e-2f3a4b5c6d7e

	measure 'League Avg Max Speed (mph)' = AVERAGE('FactEdgeBurstDetails'[SkatingSpeedDetails.maxSkatingSpeed.leagueAvg.imperial])
		formatString: 0.00
		lineageTag: 3c4d5e6f-7a8b-9c0d-1e2f-3a4b5c6d7e8f

	measure 'Player Bursts > 22mph' = SUM('FactEdgeBurstDetails'[burstsOver22])
		formatString: 0
		lineageTag: 4d5e6f7a-8b9c-0d1e-2f3a-4b5c6d7e8f9a

	measure 'Player Bursts 20-22mph' = SUM('FactEdgeBurstDetails'[bursts20To22])
		formatString: 0
		lineageTag: 5e6f7a8b-9c0d-1e2f-3a4b-5c6d7e8f9a0b

	measure 'Player Goals' = SUM('DimPlayers'[Goals])
		formatString: 0
		lineageTag: a7570938-979f-4e80-a29b-4cd7d2519b6a

	measure 'Player Assists' = SUM('DimPlayers'[Assists])
		formatString: 0
		lineageTag: 4a6c7476-e3cf-43ad-af51-77e2bd493ad9

	measure 'Player Points' = SUM('DimPlayers'[Points])
		formatString: 0
		lineageTag: a6b93a6b-824f-457e-ae21-896744b9d35a

	measure 'Games Played' = SUM('DimPlayers'[GamesPlayed])
		formatString: 0
		lineageTag: d3b4eedb-5a04-4e14-bb27-58fcbaa47ea7

	measure 'Total Games Played' =
			
			CALCULATE(
			    DISTINCTCOUNT(DimGames[GameID]),
			    DimGames[GameState] = "FINAL" || DimGames[GameState] = "OFF"
			)
		formatString: 0
		lineageTag: 69802e14-18f6-41a3-80ad-c3c667605fd1

	measure 'Team Wins' = ```
			
					VAR SelectedTeam = SELECTEDVALUE(DimTeams[TeamAbbrev])
					RETURN
					CALCULATE(
					    COUNTROWS(DimGames),
					    (DimGames[HomeTeamAbbrev] = SelectedTeam && DimGames[HomeScore] > DimGames[AwayScore]) ||
					    (DimGames[AwayTeamAbbrev] = SelectedTeam && DimGames[AwayScore] > DimGames[HomeScore])
					)
			```
		formatString: 0
		lineageTag: 94c9a502-0e3d-4c16-a153-a749ac2af8bb

	measure 'Team Losses' = ```
			
					VAR SelectedTeam = SELECTEDVALUE(DimTeams[TeamAbbrev])
					RETURN
					CALCULATE(
					    COUNTROWS(DimGames),
					    (DimGames[HomeTeamAbbrev] = SelectedTeam && DimGames[HomeScore] < DimGames[AwayScore]) ||
					    (DimGames[AwayTeamAbbrev] = SelectedTeam && DimGames[AwayScore] < DimGames[HomeScore])
					)
			```
		formatString: 0
		lineageTag: 568a9445-ea2e-460f-82c6-395178899731

	measure 'Team Ties' = ```
			
					VAR SelectedTeam = SELECTEDVALUE(DimTeams[TeamAbbrev])
					RETURN
					CALCULATE(
					    COUNTROWS(DimGames),
					    (DimGames[HomeTeamAbbrev] = SelectedTeam && DimGames[HomeScore] = DimGames[AwayScore]) ||
					    (DimGames[AwayTeamAbbrev] = SelectedTeam && DimGames[AwayScore] = DimGames[HomeScore])
					)
			```
		formatString: 0
		lineageTag: 53811775-a520-44bb-8f9d-2a8c311d30a7

	column Value
		dataType: int64
		isHidden
		lineageTag: df0fe028-898e-436c-9506-03a97af5e407
		summarizeBy: none
		isNameInferred
		sourceColumn: [Value]

	partition _Measures = calculated
		mode: import
		source = {BLANK()}

// FILE: docs\CONTEXT_DUMP.md
// --------------------------------------------------------------------------

# 🧠 NHL 2026: Platform Context

**Stack:** Power BI Desktop (TMDL Format) + Python (Code Extraction) + DAX + Power Query (M)
**Data Sources:** Live NHL Web API (`v1/gamecenter`, `v1/edge`, `v1/standings`) + Historical Kaggle Datasets (`game_plays.csv`, `game.csv`).
**Version:** v1.0.0 (Development)

## 🏗️ Architectural Pillars

### 1. The Lambda Architecture (Y-Intersection)
* **Rule:** We never force Power Query to stitch massive historical local files with live web APIs. 
* **Mechanism:** Live data (`FactLivePlays`) and Historical data (`FactHistoricalPlays`) are extracted independently in Power Query. They are merged instantly in RAM using the DAX `UNION` function (`FactPlayByPlay = UNION('FactLivePlays', 'FactHistoricalPlays')`).

### 2. Strict Star Schema
* **Rule:** Fact tables NEVER connect to other Fact tables.
* **Mechanism:** All relationships must flow strictly from Dimension tables (`DimGames`, `DimTeams`, `DimPlayers`) downstream to Fact tables (1-to-Many). Cross-filtering is single-directional unless explicitly required for a complex measure.

### 3. Memory & Performance Efficiency
* **Rule:** Keep the VertiPaq engine lean.
* **Mechanism:** * "Auto Date/Time" is strictly disabled globally.
    * All Staging queries (e.g., `Staging_EDGE`) have "Enable Load" unchecked.
    * The massive 750MB Kaggle CSV utilizes Early Filtering (>= 2021 season) to prevent RAM timeouts during development.

### 4. Explicit Data Typing
* **Rule:** No implicit type conversions. No `any` types in the final model.
* **Mechanism:** Every column in Power Query terminates with a strict `Table.TransformColumnTypes` step. IDs are `Int64.Type`, coordinates/speeds are `type number` (Decimal), and text strings are `type text`.

| `Team Goal Diff` | `_Measures` | `SUM('DimTeams'[GoalDifferential])` | Casual Fan |
| `Current Streak` | `_Measures` | Extracts streak contextually at Team hierarchy | Casual Fan |
| `Player Goals` | `_Measures` | `SUM('DimPlayers'[Goals])` | Casual Fan / Manager |
| `Player Assists` | `_Measures` | `SUM('DimPlayers'[Assists])` | Casual Fan / Manager |

| `Player Max Speed (mph)` | `_Measures` | `AVERAGE` of EDGE max speed | Fantasy Manager |
| `League Avg Max Speed` | `_Measures` | `AVERAGE` of EDGE league avg speed | Fantasy Manager |
| `Player Bursts > 22mph` | `_Measures` | `SUM` of bursts over 22mph | Fantasy Manager |
| `Player Bursts 20-22mph` | `_Measures` | `SUM` of bursts 20-22mph | Fantasy Manager |



// --------------------------------------------------------------------------
// FILE: docs\PERSONAS.md
// --------------------------------------------------------------------------

# 👥 Persona-Based Dashboard Design

Visuals and measures must pass the "Persona Check" based on the user's analytical goals and technical literacy.

## 1. The Casual Fan (High-Level)
* **Goal:** Wants to see the score, who scored, and basic team standings instantly.
* **Pain Point:** Overwhelmed by spreadsheets and complex scatter plots.
* **UX Constraint:** Big KPIs, prominent SVG team logos, simple bar charts, and clear conditional formatting (Win/Loss).

## 2. The Fantasy Manager (Mid-Level)
* **Goal:** Needs actionable intelligence to make roster decisions. Cares about player streaks, power-play time, and physical telemetry.
* **Pain Point:** Needs to compare multiple players simultaneously against a baseline.
* **UX Constraint:** Dense matrix tables, player headshots, and comparative Radar Plots (Player vs. League Average).

## 3. The Coach / Scout (Deep-Dive)
* **Goal:** Advanced tactical analysis. Wants to see spatial data, shooting tendencies, and expected goals (xG).
* **Pain Point:** Needs to filter by highly specific game states (e.g., 3rd period, down by 1 goal).
* **UX Constraint:** Rink-map SVG scatter plots, heatmaps, and complex spatial DAX filtering. Touch targets must allow for precise coordinate selection.

// FILE: docs\SCHEMA_ARCHITECTURE.md
// --------------------------------------------------------------------------

# 🗄️ Schema Architecture & Data Graph

**Storage Engine:** Power BI VertiPaq (In-Memory Columnar Database)
**Format:** TMDL (Tabular Model Definition Language)

## 1. High-Level Topology
*(Updated to reflect strict cascading filters and removal of ambiguous paths)*

```mermaid
graph TD
    DimGames --> FactPlayByPlay
    DimPlayers --> FactPlayByPlay
    
    DimTeams --> DimPlayers
    
    DimPlayers --> FactEdgeSkatingSpeeds
    DimPlayers --> FactEdgeBurstDetails
    DimGames --> FactEdgeSkatingSpeeds
```

## 2. Dimension Tables (Lookups)

### `DimGames`
* **Purpose:** Unified tracking of all games (Live API + Historical Kaggle).
* **Fields:** `GameID` (PK), `Season`, `GameType`, `GameDate`, `HomeTeamID`, `AwayTeamID`.

### `DimTeams`
* **Purpose:** The Digital Rolodex for franchises. 
* **Fields:** `TeamID` (PK), `FranchiseID`, `TeamName`, `TeamAbbrev`, `TeamLogoURL`, `Conference`, `Division`, `LeagueRank`, `Points`, `GoalDifferential`, `StreakType`, `StreakCount`.

### `DimPlayers`
* **Purpose:** Active roster dictionary.
* **Fields:** `PlayerID` (PK), `PlayerName`, `Position`, `ShootsCatches`, `GamesPlayed`, `Goals`, `Assists`, `Points`, `CurrentTeamAbbrev` (FK to DimTeams), `HeadshotURL`.

## 3. Fact Tables (Events & Telemetry)

### `FactPlayByPlay` (DAX UNION Table)
* **Purpose:** The core event ledger. Unifies `FactLivePlays` and `FactHistoricalPlays`.
* **Fields:** `GameID` (FK), `EventID`, `PeriodNumber`, `TimeInPeriod_Seconds`, `EventType`, `EventTeamID`, `X_Coord`, `Y_Coord`, `ScoringPlayerID` (FK), `ShootingPlayerID` (FK), `HittingPlayerID` (FK), `HitteePlayerID` (FK).

### `FactEdgeSkatingSpeeds`
* **Purpose:** Player telemetry for top speeds.
* **Fields:** `PlayerID` (FK), `skatingSpeed.imperial`, `skatingSpeed.metric`, `periodDescriptor.number`, `homeTeam.abbrev`.

### `FactEdgeBurstDetails`
* **Purpose:** Player telemetry for acceleration and league comparisons.
* **Fields:** `PlayerID` (FK), `SkatingSpeedDetails.maxSkatingSpeed.imperial`, `SkatingSpeedDetails.maxSkatingSpeed.leagueAvg.imperial`, `burstsOver22`, `bursts20To22`, `bursts18To20`.

## 4. DAX Measures (`_Measures` Table)
* **Purpose:** Centralized repository for all explicit DAX calculations to prevent model scattering.
* **Metrics:** Covered in `MEASURE_DICTIONARY.md`

* Will this inflate VertiPaq memory?

# 🛡️ Master Post-Sprint Audit & Sync Prompt (v1.0)

**Trigger:** Run this after completing a major Sprint or Epic, before finalizing the version.
**Goal:** Ensure the TMDL Code, the Architecture Specs, and the Project Boards are in perfect synchronization.

---

**Role:** Lead Power BI Architect & Technical Writer.

**Input:**
1. **Codebase Dump:** The complete `powerbi_codebase.txt` containing the semantic model, docs, and scripts.
2. **Context:** A brief summary of the DAX measures, M-code changes, or visual features just completed.

**Your Task:** Execute the following 3 phases in order.

### PHASE 1: Code Quality & Integrity Gate
Scan the provided `.tmdl` files for pre-release red flags:
* **Type Safety:** Are there any missing `dataType` declarations in the DAX measures or missing `Table.TransformColumnTypes` in M-code?
* **Star Schema:** Are there any bidirectional or Many-to-Many relationships that were not explicitly documented and justified?
* *Output:* PASS/FAIL with specific file and line references if issues are found.

### PHASE 2: Drift Detection (The Documentation)
Cross-reference the documentation sources of truth against the actual living code.
1. **Schema Drift (`docs/SCHEMA_ARCHITECTURE.md`):** Do the documented Fact/Dimension tables match the exact definitions and relationships in the TMDL files?
2. **Measure Drift (`docs/MEASURE_DICTIONARY.md`):** Are all newly created DAX measures documented with their logic and intended Persona?
3. **Project Management Drift (`docs/SPRINT_BOARD.md`):** Identify which active tasks are now complete in the codebase and should be moved to the completed section.

### PHASE 3: The Universal Sync Script
*Output Format:* Produce a single table summarizing the drift, followed by a **Python script** (`scripts/sync_sprint_state.py`) that overwrites all drifted markdown files in one go.

**Strict Scripting Constraints:**
* **Full Files Only:** Provide the *entire* content for the modified markdown files. No summarizing.
* **Markdown Protection (CRITICAL):** Because Markdown files contain code blocks, define `FENCE = chr(96) * 3` at the top of the Python script. Use `__FENCE__` as a placeholder in your raw Python string. Use `.replace('__FENCE__', FENCE)` during the file-writing block to safely write the files.

---
**Reply:** 'NHL Audit Engine Loaded. Awaiting Full Codebase and Sprint Summary to begin the Post-Sprint Sync.'


// --------------------------------------------------------------------------
// FILE: scripts\extract_pbi_code.py
// --------------------------------------------------------------------------

import os
import glob

def main():
    # 1. Define paths relative to this script
    script_dir = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))
    project_root = os.path.abspath(os.path.join(script_dir, '..'))
    output_file = os.path.join(project_root, 'powerbi_codebase.txt')

    files_to_export = []

    # 2. Dynamically find the SemanticModel directory for TMDL files
    semantic_model_dirs = glob.glob(os.path.join(project_root, '*.SemanticModel'))
    if semantic_model_dirs:
        semantic_model_dir = semantic_model_dirs[0]
        definition_dir = os.path.join(semantic_model_dir, 'definition')
        if os.path.exists(definition_dir):
            tmdl_files = glob.glob(os.path.join(definition_dir, '**', '*.tmdl'), recursive=True)
            files_to_export.extend(tmdl_files)
            print(f"🔍 Found {len(tmdl_files)} TMDL files.")
        else:
            print(f"⚠️ Warning: 'definition' folder not found inside {os.path.basename(semantic_model_dir)}.")
    else:
        print("⚠️ Warning: No .SemanticModel directory found. Ensure this is a .pbip project.")

    # 3. Collect Documentation Files
    docs_dir = os.path.join(project_root, 'docs')
    if os.path.exists(docs_dir):
        doc_files = glob.glob(os.path.join(docs_dir, '**', '*.md'), recursive=True)
        doc_files.extend(glob.glob(os.path.join(docs_dir, '**', '*.txt'), recursive=True))
        files_to_export.extend(doc_files)
        print(f"🔍 Found {len(doc_files)} Documentation files.")
    else:
        print("⚠️ Warning: 'docs' directory not found.")

    # 4. Collect Script Files
    scripts_dir = os.path.join(project_root, 'scripts')
    if os.path.exists(scripts_dir):
        script_files = glob.glob(os.path.join(scripts_dir, '**', '*.py'), recursive=True)
        # Exclude the output file if it accidentally gets caught or placed here
        script_files = [f for f in script_files if not f.endswith('powerbi_codebase.txt')]
        files_to_export.extend(script_files)
        print(f"🔍 Found {len(script_files)} Script files.")
    else:
        print("⚠️ Warning: 'scripts' directory not found.")

    if not files_to_export:
        print("❌ Error: No files found to export.")
        return

    # 5. Read and stitch files together
    print(f"\n📦 Compiling {len(files_to_export)} total files into {os.path.basename(output_file)}...")
    
    with open(output_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as outfile:
        outfile.write("=== POWER BI PROJECT FULL EXPORT ===\n")
        outfile.write("This file contains the complete TMDL data model, project documentation, and automation scripts.\n")
        outfile.write("=" * 80 + "\n\n")

        for file_path in files_to_export:
            # Get a clean relative path to use as the file header
            relative_path = os.path.relpath(file_path, project_root)
            
            outfile.write(f"// {'-' * 74}\n")
            outfile.write(f"// FILE: {relative_path}\n")
            outfile.write(f"// {'-' * 74}\n\n")
            
            try:
                # 'utf-8-sig' handles the Byte Order Mark (BOM) that Microsoft tools often add
                with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8-sig') as infile:
                    content = infile.read()
                    outfile.write(content)
            except Exception as e:
                outfile.write(f"// [ERROR READING FILE: {e}]\n")
            
            outfile.write("\n\n\n")

    print(f"✅ Success! Full codebase exported to: {output_file}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

import os

def sync_docs():
    script_dir = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))

    files_to_update = {}

    # --- FILE 1: SPRINT_BOARD.md ---
    files_to_update['docs/SPRINT_BOARD.md'] = r"""# 🏃 Active Sprint Board

**Current Phase:** Sprint 2.0 (Advanced Analytics & EDGE)

## ✅ Completed Sprints
- [x] **Sprint 0.1 - 0.3:** Data plumbing, Lambda architecture, and PK hardening.
- [x] **Sprint 1.0: The Core Reporting Flow.** - [x] PROJ-01: Standings Matrix
  - [x] PROJ-02: League Dashboard
  - [x] PROJ-03: Team Report (Drill-through base)
  - [x] PROJ-04: Player Scorecard (Target page)

## 🟡 Sprint 2.0: Advanced Analytics (Active)
- [ ] **PROJ-05: The EDGE Radar Plot.** Re-integrate burst telemetry DAX measures into the Player Scorecard.
- [ ] **PROJ-06: Spatial Rink Mapping.** Configure the custom SVG visual to plot `X_Coord` and `Y_Coord` from `FactPlayByPlay`.

## 🧊 Product Backlog (Sprint 3.0)
- [ ] **PROJ-07:** Expected Goals (xG) Distance DAX Model.
- [ ] **PROJ-08:** Trade Target Scatter Plot (Speed vs. Volume).
"""

    # --- FILE 2: ROADMAP.md ---
    files_to_update['docs/ROADMAP.md'] = r"""# 🗺️ NHL Analytics Product Roadmap

## 📅 Q2 2026: The Core Modules
| Status | ID | Epic Name | Persona Focus | Description |
| :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- |
| ✅ **Complete** | `EPIC-01` | **The Core Reporting Flow** | Casual Fan / Manager | Establish the Macro-to-Micro drill-through experience (League -> Team -> Player) using traditional box-score metrics. |
| 🟡 **Active** | `EPIC-02` | **The Fantasy Console (EDGE)** | Fantasy Manager | Deploy EDGE telemetry radar plots and speed scatter charts. |
| ⚪ Planned | `EPIC-03` | **The Coach's War Room** | Scout | Build the Expected Goals (xG) spatial engine using X/Y coordinates. |
| ⚪ Planned | `EPIC-04` | **Automated Deployment** | Admin | Migrate to Power BI Service with scheduled daily API refreshes. |
"""

    for relative_path, content in files_to_update.items():
        full_path = os.path.join(project_root, relative_path)
        if os.path.exists(full_path):
            safe_content = content.replace('__FENCE__', FENCE)
            with open(full_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                f.write(safe_content)
            print(f"✅ Synced: {relative_path}")

    print("\n🚀 Post-Sprint Audit complete. Sprint 1.0 is officially closed.")
